CREATE TABLE hearing (hearing_id INT PRIMARY KEY, hearing_date DATE, case_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (case_id) REFERENCES case(case_id))

CREATE TABLE document (document_id INT PRIMARY KEY, document_name STRING, case_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (case_id) REFERENCES case(case_id))</t><s>alter table client add column email string</s>
